     577                 :           0 : static double calc_frame_boost(const PRIMARY_RATE_CONTROL *p_rc,

     583                 :           0 :                                             frame_info->bit_depth);

     602                 :           0 :   return AOMMIN(frame_boost, max_boost * boost_q_correction);

     758                 :             : // Calculate a section intra ratio used in setting max loop filter.

    1352                 :             :     // Check mean and variance of stats in a window
    1353                 :           0 :     double mean_intra = 0.001, var_intra = 0.001;

    1431                 :           0 : static void adjust_unstable_region_bounds(const FIRSTPASS_STATS *stats,

    1441                 :             :   // overall the performance is not very sensitive to small changes to them.

    1450                 :             :                                 regions[k - 1].start + 1);

    1473                 :           0 :         }
    1474                 :           0 :       }

    2748                 :             : #define ERROR_SPIKE 5.0
    2749                 :             : 
    2750                 :             : // Slide show transition detection.
    2751                 :             : // Tests for case where there is very low error either side of the current frame
    2752                 :             : // but much higher just for this frame. This can help detect key frames in
    2753                 :             : // slide shows even where the slides are pictures of different sizes.
    2754                 :             : // Also requires that intra and inter errors are very similar to help eliminate
    2755                 :             : // harmful false positives.

    2762                 :           0 :          (this_frame->coded_error > (next_frame->coded_error * ERROR_SPIKE));
    2763                 :             : }
